This series was originally planned for the fall of 1984, Mondays at 8:00PM Eastern/7:00PM Central. However, ABC executives changed their minds when the summer series Call to Glory did well, and Street Hawk was pushed to mid-season. Street Hawk made its debut on January 4, 1985 on ABC at 9:00PM Eastern/8:00PM Central and ran until May 16, 1985.\n\nReruns aired on the USA Network on Saturdays at 10:00AM from 1990-91.", "poster_path": "/r3bajIlqFrqcd4aztq8E2Dcouur.jpg", "media_type": "tv", "adult": false, "original_language": "en", "genre_ids": [10759, 9648, 10765, 18], "popularity": 3.4139, "first_air_date": "1985-01-04", "vote_average": 6.8, "vote_count": 94, "origin_country": ["US"]}]}]}
